```

(   )---(   )   (   )   (   )---(   )---(w 3)---(   )   (   )---(b 2)   (b 2)---(   )   (   )---(b 2)   (   )---(   )   (   )   (   )---(   )   (b 3)---(   )---(   )   (   )---(   )---(   )---(   )---(b14)
```
